If you have recurring errors, we recommend that you try to login or register with a laptop or desktop./n/nCommon browser issues:/nPlease ensure that you are using a Google Chrome browser if you are on a Windows device or Safari if you are using an Apple device. You might want to try an incognito tab on the Google Chrome browser if you are still having issues./nThe password needs to be a minimum of 8 characters, including 1 uppercase character, 1 numeric digit and 1 special character (eg ! #) /nPlease note that @, ' and ' will not be accepted as special characters. /n/nIt may be useful to clear the cache on your browser as we have found that this can sometimes hinder a login or registration. /nGoogle Chrome:/nAt the top right of your Google Chrome browser, click the 3 ellipses and select ?Settings?./nScroll down to see the word ?Advanced? and click on this./nOn the ?Privacy and Security? box, click ?Clear Browsing Data? and then select the period of time you wish to clear (the default is set as 4 weeks) and then click ?Clear Data?./nSafari:/nClick on the Safari drop down menu and select Preferences/nClick the Advanced tab. Please check that you have completed all required sections and if you are not sure, please send us a screenshot so that we can check for you./nThe previous employment and references section requires a minimum number to be completed before this section is marked as ?complete? i.e for Professional Services job, at least 2 references are required and for Academic roles, at least 3 is required./nAlso, the Professional Registrations sections is mandatory even if user does not hold any ? when they complete this section, there is an option to select ?not applicable?./n/nA common issue when completing the previous employment section is exceeding the maximum character length - please check the number of characters in the sections below:/n/nShort summary of main duties field: 2000 character limit (including spaces)/nReason for leaving field: 200 character limit (including spaces)/n/nThe system should stop you inputting past this max point but on some browsers it lets you exceed this limit.  When attempting to save the page, an error message is displayed./nShould you be unsure as to whether you have exceeded this limit, please provide the text you are trying to input so that we can test this for you./n/nWhen adding information for an application on the Recruitment portal, the following file types will be accepted: .doc, docx, .odt, .pdf, .rtf, .xls. .xlsx /n /nPlease note that users cannot use the following characters when naming their files: /n # % & { } $ ! ' @ /n /nThe maximum size per file that will be accepted is 5mb and the file name should not exceed 30 characters  /n/nKind Regards," id='INSRES'>HR - DS - Recruit troubleshooting</option>

Go to Settings. /n? Tap Personal Hotspot. /n? Toggle Personal Hotspot On by tapping the button. /n? Using the device you want to connect with, scan for the Wi-Fi hotspot network, and enter the password when prompted. The password is automatically generated, but you can change it with a tap. There is no option to change the Wi-Fi network name as it?s linked to the name of your device. /n/nHow to set up Wi-Fi tether on Android /n/nYou can use your phone's mobile data to connect another phone, tablet or computer to the Internet. Sharing a connection this way is called tethering or using a hotspot. Some phones can share Wi-Fi connection by tethering. /n/nImportant: Some mobile operators limit or charge extra for tethering. We recommend checking with your operator. /n/nImportant: While it is easy to set up tethering, there is an added wrinkle for Android ? the user interface is not the same for every device. That means we can?t provide exact steps for every device. /n/nSome of these steps work only on Android 9 and up. /n/nTurn on your hotspot 1. Swipe down from the top of the screen. /n2. Tap Hotspot . /n? If you don?t find Hotspot , at the bottom left, tap Edit and drag Hotspot into your Quick Settings. /n/n---------------------------- OR -------------------------------------------------- /n/n? Go to Settings > Connections. /n/n? Tap Mobile Hotspot and Tethering. /n/n? Tap Mobile Hotspot. /n/n? Note the network name and password. /n/n? Toggle Mobile Hotspot On./n/nChoose how to tether Tether by Wi-Fi /n/n1. Swipe down from the top of the screen. /n/n2. Touch and hold Hotspot . /n/n3. Turn on Wi-Fi hotspot. Tip: To find or change your hotspot name or password, tap it. You may need to first tap Set up Wi-Fi hotspot. /n/nConnect another device to your phone's hotspot /n/n1. On the other device, open that device's list of Wi-Fi options. /n/n2. Pick your phone's hotspot name. /n/n3. Enter your phone's hotspot password. /n/n4. Click Connect. /n/nIf you don't want your hotspot to require a password: /n/n1. Swipe down from the top of the screen. /n/n2. Touch and hold Hotspot . /n/n3. Under 'Security', tap None. Tip: You can share your phone's mobile data with up to 10 other devices via a Wi-Fi hotspot." id='INSRES'>NLR Project (IN CHANGE WINDOW) - Customer Resolution</option>

<option title="Resi - Cancellation enquiry$$ Thank you for contacting King's Residences/n/nDepending on where you are in the bookings process, cancellation terms will vary:/n /n1) If you have booked a room and want to cancel after the 10th June (2022) deadline, you will loose your £450.00 pre-payment. You can cancel in your portal using the 'cancel' button./n/n2) If you have booked a room and want to cancel after the 10th June deadline and the contract start date has passed (but you have not moved in), you will loose your £450.00 pre-payment and be charged an additional 4 weeks rent. We will refund the £450.00 in these circumstances. If you have already checked into your accommodation the rent pre-payment will not be refunded and you will be liable for the fee until the next Saturday of your check out date or withdrawal confirmation date (whichever comes last). You are only allowed to stay for a maximum of 2 weeks from the date of the withdrawal confirmation/n/nPlease see our full cancellation matrix online here: https://www.kcl.ac.uk/accommodation/assets/policies/cancellation-policy-22-23.pdf/n/nPlease don't hesitate to contact us back should you have any further queries./n/nKind Regards/n/nKing's Residences/nEstates and Facilities Directorate/nKing's College London  /nTel: +44 (0)20 7848 5959/nEmail: kingsresidences@kcl.ac.uk/n/nWorld class services for a world class university  /n/nPlease see our updated FAQ for any information about COVID19 and self-isolation in the residences:/nhttps://www.kcl.ac.uk/accommodation/covid-19-updates" id='INSRES'>Resi - Cancellation enquiry</option>

<option title="Resi - COVID report self-isolation$$ Thank you for contacting King's Residences and letting us know about your need to self isolate. /n/nIf you have not already done so, please immediately fill in the University self-isolation reporting form so that we can arrange the necessary support for you:/n/nhttps://www.kcl.ac.uk/coronavirus/form/n/nIf you need to quarantine or self-isolate it means that you must stay in your room and only interact with others online or by phone, even those in your flat (household)./n/nWe know this will be hard but it is really important to protect the other people you are living with and those in the community./n/n- You need to stay in your room for the quarantine/self-isolation period./n- You cannot go to the shops or go outside, even for exercise./n- You will need to order food and groceries online which the residences team will bring to your door./n- You are able to use the kitchen during this period but you must be alone in the kitchen, wear a face covering, sanitise the work areas before and after use, do not share utensils, cutlery or crockery, and take food back to your room to eat./n- The residences team will check in with you regularly either online or by phone./n/nYou will still be able to take part in online teaching, activities and access our services whilst you are quarantining/self-isolating./n/nAll students in a King's residence who need to quarantine will be provided with the appropriate support such as assistance with food provision and deliveries brought to flats./n/nPlease do reach out to your welfare leads for support if you need them, you can find all of their contact details online here:/n/nhttps://www.kcl.ac.uk/accommodation/living-with-us/welfare/n/nIf there is anything more you need, please do let us know./n/nWarm Regards/n/nThe Residences Team" id='INSRES'>Resi - COVID report self-isolation</option>
